\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga872d16e4c77f58c0436f356255920cfc}{glfw\+Poll\+Events}} (\mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}})
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Processes all pending events. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga6e042d05823c11e11c7339b81a237738}{glfw\+Wait\+Events}} (\mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}})
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Waits until events are queued and processes them. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga05223a0a4c5e50f10f289e60398153aa}{glfw\+Wait\+Events\+Timeout}} (double timeout)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Waits with timeout until events are queued and processes them. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_gad6f6b997278c91c43b35970eb9713d7e}{glfw\+Post\+Empty\+Event}} (\mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}})
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Posts an empty event to the event queue. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_gafb827800eedbfcbc97b1e5408df668d7}{glfw\+Swap\+Buffers}} (\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\mbox{\hyperlink{joysticks_8c_a80de27bd7dc4e2b2ad3d5895b97a70f0}{window}})
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Swaps the front and back buffers of the specified window. \end{DoxyCompactList}\end{DoxyCompactItemize}


\doxysubsection{详细描述}
Functions and types related to windows. 

This is the reference documentation for window related functions and types, including creation, deletion and event polling. For more task-\/oriented information, see the \doxysectlink{window_guide}{Window guide}{0}.

\end{DoxyCode}

\doxysubsection{函数说明}
\Hypertarget{group__window_gaaccd00fafe81e2db94e8cdf55721e055}\index{Window reference@{Window reference}!glfwCreateWindow@{glfwCreateWindow}}
\index{glfwCreateWindow@{glfwCreateWindow}!Window reference@{Window reference}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwCreateWindow()}{glfwCreateWindow()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_gaaccd00fafe81e2db94e8cdf55721e055} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} glfw\+Create\+Window (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}}}]{width}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}}}]{height}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{title}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__monitor_ga8d9efd1cde9426692c73fe40437d0ae3}{GLFWmonitor}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{monitor}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{share}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Creates a window and its associated context. 

This function creates a window and its associated Open\+GL or Open\+GL ES context. Most of the options controlling how the window and its context should be created are specified with \doxysectlink{window_guide_window_hints}{window hints}{2}.

Successful creation does not change which context is current. Before you can use the newly created context, you need to \doxysectlink{context_guide_context_current}{make it current}{1}. For information about the {\ttfamily share} parameter, see \doxysectlink{context_guide_context_sharing}{Context object sharing}{2}.

The created window, framebuffer and context may differ from what you requested, as not all parameters and hints are \doxysectlink{window_guide_window_hints_hard}{hard constraints}{3}. This includes the size of the window, especially for full screen windows. To query the actual attributes of the created window, framebuffer and context, see \doxylink{group__window_ga1bb0c7e100418e284dbb800789c63d40}{glfw\+Get\+Window\+Attrib}, \doxylink{group__window_ga7feb769ebb3f3d21579b5a3fb07be76e}{glfw\+Get\+Window\+Size} and \doxylink{group__window_gaf7d17f3534b4b6dc9a6f905e3a240b7e}{glfw\+Get\+Framebuffer\+Size}.

To create a full screen window, you need to specify the monitor the window will cover. If no monitor is specified, the window will be windowed mode. Unless you have a way for the user to choose a specific monitor, it is recommended that you pick the primary monitor. For more information on how to query connected monitors, see \doxysectlink{monitor_guide_monitor_monitors}{Retrieving monitors}{2}.

For full screen windows, the specified size becomes the resolution of the window\textquotesingle{}s {\itshape desired video mode}. As long as a full screen window is not iconified, the supported video mode most closely matching the desired video mode is set for the specified monitor. For more information about full screen windows, including the creation of so called {\itshape windowed full screen} or {\itshape borderless full screen} windows, see \doxysectlink{window_guide_window_windowed_full_screen}{"{}\+Windowed full screen"{} windows}{3}.

Once you have created the window, you can switch it between windowed and full screen mode with \doxylink{group__window_ga12fabf78575e59c00f822f323ae0b6ae}{glfw\+Set\+Window\+Monitor}. This will not affect its Open\+GL or Open\+GL ES context.

By default, newly created windows use the placement recommended by the window system. To create the window at a specific position, set the \doxylink{window_guide_GLFW_POSITION_X}{GLFW\+\_\+\+POSITION\+\_\+X} and \doxylink{window_guide_GLFW_POSITION_Y}{GLFW\+\_\+\+POSITION\+\_\+Y} window hints before creation. To restore the default behavior, set either or both hints back to {\ttfamily GLFW\+\_\+\+ANY\+\_\+\+POSITION}.

As long as at least one full screen window is not iconified, the screensaver is prohibited from starting.

Window systems put limits on window sizes. Very large or very small window dimensions may be overridden by the window system on creation. Check the actual \doxysectlink{window_guide_window_size}{size}{2} after creation.

The \doxysectlink{window_guide_buffer_swap}{swap interval}{1} is not set during window creation and the initial value may vary depending on driver settings and defaults.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em width} & The desired width, in screen coordinates, of the window. This must be greater than zero. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em height} & The desired height, in screen coordinates, of the window. This must be greater than zero. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em title} & The initial, UTF-\/8 encoded window title. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em monitor} & The monitor to use for full screen mode, or {\ttfamily NULL} for windowed mode. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em share} & The window whose context to share resources with, or {\ttfamily NULL} to not share resources. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
The handle of the created window, or {\ttfamily NULL} if an \doxysectlink{intro_guide_error_handling}{error}{1} occurred.
\end{DoxyReturn}
@errors Possible errors include \doxylink{group__errors_ga2374ee02c177f12e1fa76ff3ed15e14a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group__errors_ga76f6bb9c4eea73db675f096b404593ce}{GLFW\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+ENUM}, \doxylink{group__errors_gaaf2ef9aa8202c2b82ac2d921e554c687}{GLFW\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}, \doxylink{group__errors_ga56882b290db23261cc6c053c40c2d08e}{GLFW\+\_\+\+API\+\_\+\+UNAVAILABLE}, \doxylink{group__errors_gad16c5565b4a69f9c2a9ac2c0dbc89462}{GLFW\+\_\+\+VERSION\+\_\+\+UNAVAILABLE}, \doxylink{group__errors_ga196e125ef261d94184e2b55c05762f14}{GLFW\+\_\+\+FORMAT\+\_\+\+UNAVAILABLE}, \doxylink{group__errors_gacff24d2757da752ae4c80bf452356487}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NO\+\_\+\+WINDOW\+\_\+\+CONTEXT} and \doxylink{group__errors_gad44162d78100ea5e87cdd38426b8c7a1}{GLFW\+\_\+\+PLATFORM\+\_\+\+ERROR}.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{备注}
@win32 Window creation will fail if the Microsoft GDI software Open\+GL implementation is the only one available.

@win32 If the executable has an icon resource named {\ttfamily GLFW\+\_\+\+ICON,} it will be set as the initial icon for the window. If no such icon is present, the {\ttfamily IDI\+\_\+\+APPLICATION} icon will be used instead. To set a different icon, see \doxylink{group__window_ga182987a1a62a41a924842b9473d560df}{glfw\+Set\+Window\+Icon}.

@win32 The context to share resources with must not be current on any other thread.

@macos The OS only supports core profile contexts for Open\+GL versions 3.\+2 and later. Before creating an Open\+GL context of version 3.\+2 or later you must set the \doxylink{window_guide_GLFW_OPENGL_PROFILE_hint}{GLFW\+\_\+\+OPENGL\+\_\+\+PROFILE} hint accordingly. Open\+GL 3.\+0 and 3.\+1 contexts are not supported at all on mac\+OS.

@macos The GLFW window has no icon, as it is not a document window, but the dock icon will be the same as the application bundle\textquotesingle{}s icon. For more information on bundles, see the \href{https://developer.apple.com/library/mac/documentation/CoreFoundation/Conceptual/CFBundles/}{\texttt{ Bundle Programming Guide}} in the Mac Developer Library.

@macos The window frame will not be rendered at full resolution on Retina displays unless the \doxylink{window_guide_GLFW_SCALE_FRAMEBUFFER_hint}{GLFW\+\_\+\+SCALE\+\_\+\+FRAMEBUFFER} hint is {\ttfamily GLFW\+\_\+\+TRUE} and the {\ttfamily NSHigh\+Resolution\+Capable} key is enabled in the application bundle\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily Info.\+plist}. For more information, see \href{https://developer.apple.com/library/mac/documentation/GraphicsAnimation/Conceptual/HighResolutionOSX/Explained/Explained.html}{\texttt{ High Resolution Guidelines for OS X}} in the Mac Developer Library. The GLFW test and example programs use a custom {\ttfamily Info.\+plist} template for this, which can be found as {\ttfamily CMake/\+Info.\+plist.\+in} in the source tree.

@macos When activating frame autosaving with \doxylink{window_guide_GLFW_COCOA_FRAME_NAME_hint}{GLFW\+\_\+\+COCOA\+\_\+\+FRAME\+\_\+\+NAME}, the specified window size and position may be overridden by previously saved values.

@wayland GLFW uses \href{https://gitlab.freedesktop.org/libdecor/libdecor}{\texttt{ libdecor}} where available to create its window decorations. This in turn uses server-\/side XDG decorations where available and provides high quality client-\/side decorations on compositors like GNOME. If both XDG decorations and libdecor are unavailable, GLFW falls back to a very simple set of window decorations that only support moving, resizing and the window manager\textquotesingle{}s right-\/click menu.

@x11 Some window managers will not respect the placement of initially hidden windows.

@x11 Due to the asynchronous nature of X11, it may take a moment for a window to reach its requested state. This means you may not be able to query the final size, position or other attributes directly after window creation.

@x11 The class part of the {\ttfamily WM\+\_\+\+CLASS} window property will by default be set to the window title passed to this function. The instance part will use the contents of the {\ttfamily RESOURCE\+\_\+\+NAME} environment variable, if present and not empty, or fall back to the window title. Set the \doxylink{window_guide_GLFW_X11_CLASS_NAME_hint}{GLFW\+\_\+\+X11\+\_\+\+CLASS\+\_\+\+NAME} and \doxylink{window_guide_GLFW_X11_INSTANCE_NAME_hint}{GLFW\+\_\+\+X11\+\_\+\+INSTANCE\+\_\+\+NAME} window hints to override this.
\end{DoxyRemark}
@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
\doxysectlink{window_guide_window_creation}{Window creation}{2} 

\doxylink{group__window_ga806747476b7247d292be3711c323ea10}{glfw\+Destroy\+Window}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxySince}{自从}
Added in version 3.\+0. Replaces {\ttfamily glfw\+Open\+Window}.
\end{DoxySince}
This function creates a window and its associated Open\+GL or Open\+GL ES context. Most of the options controlling how the window and its context should be created are specified with \doxysectlink{window_guide_window_hints}{window hints}{2}.

Successful creation does not change which context is current. Before you can use the newly created context, you need to \doxysectlink{context_guide_context_current}{make it current}{1}. For information about the {\ttfamily share} parameter, see \doxysectlink{context_guide_context_sharing}{Context object sharing}{2}.

The created window, framebuffer and context may differ from what you requested, as not all parameters and hints are \doxysectlink{window_guide_window_hints_hard}{hard constraints}{3}. This includes the size of the window, especially for full screen windows. To query the actual attributes of the created window, framebuffer and context, see \doxylink{group__window_ga1bb0c7e100418e284dbb800789c63d40}{glfw\+Get\+Window\+Attrib}, \doxylink{group__window_ga7feb769ebb3f3d21579b5a3fb07be76e}{glfw\+Get\+Window\+Size} and \doxylink{group__window_gaf7d17f3534b4b6dc9a6f905e3a240b7e}{glfw\+Get\+Framebuffer\+Size}.

To create a full screen window, you need to specify the monitor the window will cover. If no monitor is specified, the window will be windowed mode. Unless you have a way for the user to choose a specific monitor, it is recommended that you pick the primary monitor. For more information on how to query connected monitors, see \doxysectlink{monitor_guide_monitor_monitors}{Retrieving monitors}{2}.

For full screen windows, the specified size becomes the resolution of the window\textquotesingle{}s {\itshape desired video mode}. As long as a full screen window is not iconified, the supported video mode most closely matching the desired video mode is set for the specified monitor. For more information about full screen windows, including the creation of so called {\itshape windowed full screen} or {\itshape borderless full screen} windows, see \doxysectlink{window_guide_window_windowed_full_screen}{"{}\+Windowed full screen"{} windows}{3}.

By default, newly created windows use the placement recommended by the window system. To create the window at a specific position, make it initially invisible using the \doxysectlink{window_guide_window_hints_wnd}{GLFW\+\_\+\+VISIBLE}{3} window hint, set its \doxysectlink{window_guide_window_pos}{position}{2} and then \doxysectlink{window_guide_window_hide}{show}{2} it.

As long as at least one full screen window is not iconified, the screensaver is prohibited from starting.

Window systems put limits on window sizes. Very large or very small window dimensions may be overridden by the window system on creation. Check the actual \doxysectlink{window_guide_window_size}{size}{2} after creation.

The \doxysectlink{window_guide_buffer_swap}{swap interval}{1} is not set during window creation and the initial value may vary depending on driver settings and defaults.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em width} & The desired width, in screen coordinates, of the window. This must be greater than zero. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em height} & The desired height, in screen coordinates, of the window. This must be greater than zero. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em title} & The initial, UTF-\/8 encoded window title. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em monitor} & The monitor to use for full screen mode, or {\ttfamily NULL} for windowed mode. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em share} & The window whose context to share resources with, or {\ttfamily NULL} to not share resources. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
The handle of the created window, or {\ttfamily NULL} if an \doxysectlink{intro_guide_error_handling}{error}{1} occurred.
\end{DoxyReturn}
@errors Possible errors include \doxylink{group__errors_ga2374ee02c177f12e1fa76ff3ed15e14a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group__errors_ga76f6bb9c4eea73db675f096b404593ce}{GLFW\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+ENUM}, \doxylink{group__errors_gaaf2ef9aa8202c2b82ac2d921e554c687}{GLFW\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}, \doxylink{group__errors_ga56882b290db23261cc6c053c40c2d08e}{GLFW\+\_\+\+API\+\_\+\+UNAVAILABLE}, \doxylink{group__errors_gad16c5565b4a69f9c2a9ac2c0dbc89462}{GLFW\+\_\+\+VERSION\+\_\+\+UNAVAILABLE}, \doxylink{group__errors_ga196e125ef261d94184e2b55c05762f14}{GLFW\+\_\+\+FORMAT\+\_\+\+UNAVAILABLE} and \doxylink{group__errors_gad44162d78100ea5e87cdd38426b8c7a1}{GLFW\+\_\+\+PLATFORM\+\_\+\+ERROR}.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{备注}
@win32 Window creation will fail if the Microsoft GDI software Open\+GL implementation is the only one available.

@win32 If the executable has an icon resource named {\ttfamily GLFW\+\_\+\+ICON,} it will be set as the icon for the window. If no such icon is present, the {\ttfamily IDI\+\_\+\+WINLOGO} icon will be used instead.

@win32 The context to share resources with must not be current on any other thread.

@osx The GLFW window has no icon, as it is not a document window, but the dock icon will be the same as the application bundle\textquotesingle{}s icon. For more information on bundles, see the \href{https://developer.apple.com/library/mac/documentation/CoreFoundation/Conceptual/CFBundles/}{\texttt{ Bundle Programming Guide}} in the Mac Developer Library.

@osx The first time a window is created the menu bar is populated with common commands like Hide, Quit and About. The About entry opens a minimal about dialog with information from the application\textquotesingle{}s bundle. The menu bar can be disabled with a compile-\/time option.

@osx On OS X 10.\+10 and later the window frame will not be rendered at full resolution on Retina displays unless the {\ttfamily NSHigh\+Resolution\+Capable} key is enabled in the application bundle\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily Info.\+plist}. For more information, see \href{https://developer.apple.com/library/mac/documentation/GraphicsAnimation/Conceptual/HighResolutionOSX/Explained/Explained.html}{\texttt{ High Resolution Guidelines for OS X}} in the Mac Developer Library. The GLFW test and example programs use a custom {\ttfamily Info.\+plist} template for this, which can be found as {\ttfamily CMake/\+Mac\+OSXBundle\+Info.\+plist.\+in} in the source tree.

@x11 There is no mechanism for setting the window icon yet.

@x11 Some window managers will not respect the placement of initially hidden windows.

@x11 Due to the asynchronous nature of X11, it may take a moment for a window to reach its requested state. This means you may not be able to query the final size, position or other attributes directly after window creation.
\end{DoxyRemark}
@reentrancy This function must not be called from a callback.

@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwDefaultWindowHints()}{glfwDefaultWindowHints()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_ga8050ddceed9dc6bd9d3aa35666195cd4} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}} glfw\+Default\+Window\+Hints (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}}}]{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\Hypertarget{group__window_ga806747476b7247d292be3711c323ea10}\index{Window reference@{Window reference}!glfwDestroyWindow@{glfwDestroyWindow}}
\index{glfwDestroyWindow@{glfwDestroyWindow}!Window reference@{Window reference}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwDestroyWindow()}{glfwDestroyWindow()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_ga806747476b7247d292be3711c323ea10} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}} glfw\+Destroy\+Window (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{window}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Destroys the specified window and its context. 

This function destroys the specified window and its context. On calling this function, no further callbacks will be called for that window.

If the context of the specified window is current on the main thread, it is detached before being destroyed.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em window} & The window to destroy.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
@errors Possible errors include \doxylink{group__errors_ga2374ee02c177f12e1fa76ff3ed15e14a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED} and \doxylink{group__errors_gad44162d78100ea5e87cdd38426b8c7a1}{GLFW\+\_\+\+PLATFORM\+\_\+\+ERROR}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
The context of the specified window must not be current on any other thread when this function is called.
\end{DoxyNote}
@reentrancy This function must not be called from a callback.

@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}

\Hypertarget{group__window_ga0da0e3daaa2d100f44a115c09077b510}\index{Window reference@{Window reference}!glfwFocusWindow@{glfwFocusWindow}}
\index{glfwFocusWindow@{glfwFocusWindow}!Window reference@{Window reference}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwFocusWindow()}{glfwFocusWindow()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_ga0da0e3daaa2d100f44a115c09077b510} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}} glfw\+Focus\+Window (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{window}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Brings the specified window to front and sets input focus. 

This function brings the specified window to front and sets input focus. The window should already be visible and not iconified.

By default, both windowed and full screen mode windows are focused when initially created. Set the \doxylink{window_guide_GLFW_FOCUSED_hint}{GLFW\+\_\+\+FOCUSED} to disable this behavior.

Also by default, windowed mode windows are focused when shown with \doxylink{group__window_ga7945bcdff9e5e058cf36505d6873ed8c}{glfw\+Show\+Window}. Set the \doxylink{window_guide_GLFW_FOCUS_ON_SHOW_hint}{GLFW\+\_\+\+FOCUS\+\_\+\+ON\+\_\+\+SHOW} to disable this behavior.

{\bfseries{Do not use this function}} to steal focus from other applications unless you are certain that is what the user wants. Focus stealing can be extremely disruptive.

For a less disruptive way of getting the user\textquotesingle{}s attention, see \doxysectlink{window_guide_window_attention}{attention requests}{2}.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em window} & The window to give input focus.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
@errors Possible errors include \doxylink{group__errors_ga2374ee02c177f12e1fa76ff3ed15e14a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED} and \doxylink{group__errors_gad44162d78100ea5e87cdd38426b8c7a1}{GLFW\+\_\+\+PLATFORM\+\_\+\+ERROR}.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{备注}
@wayland The compositor will likely ignore focus requests unless another window created by the same application already has input focus.
\end{DoxyRemark}
@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
\doxysectlink{window_guide_window_focus}{Window input focus}{2} 

\doxysectlink{window_guide_window_attention}{Window attention request}{2}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\end{DoxySince}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwGetFramebufferSize()}{glfwGetFramebufferSize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_gaf7d17f3534b4b6dc9a6f905e3a240b7e} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}} glfw\+Get\+Framebuffer\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{window}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{width}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{height}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Retrieves the size of the framebuffer of the specified window. 

This function retrieves the size, in pixels, of the framebuffer of the specified window. If you wish to retrieve the size of the window in screen coordinates, see \doxylink{group__window_ga7feb769ebb3f3d21579b5a3fb07be76e}{glfw\+Get\+Window\+Size}.

\hline

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwGetWindowAttrib()}{glfwGetWindowAttrib()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_ga1bb0c7e100418e284dbb800789c63d40} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}} glfw\+Get\+Window\+Attrib (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{window}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}}}]{attrib}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns an attribute of the specified window. 

This function returns the value of an attribute of the specified window or its Open\+GL or Open\+GL ES context.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em window} & The window to query. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em attrib} & The \doxysectlink{window_guide_window_attribs}{window attribute}{2} whose value to return. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
The value of the attribute, or zero if an \doxysectlink{intro_guide_error_handling}{error}{1} occurred.
\end{DoxyReturn}
@errors Possible errors include \doxylink{group__errors_ga2374ee02c177f12e1fa76ff3ed15e14a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group__errors_ga76f6bb9c4eea73db675f096b404593ce}{GLFW\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+ENUM} and \doxylink{group__errors_gad44162d78100ea5e87cdd38426b8c7a1}{GLFW\+\_\+\+PLATFORM\+\_\+\+ERROR}.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{备注}
Framebuffer related hints are not window attributes. See \doxysectlink{window_guide_window_attribs_fb}{Framebuffer related attributes}{3} for more information.

Zero is a valid value for many window and context related attributes so you cannot use a return value of zero as an indication of errors. However, this function should not fail as long as it is passed valid arguments and the library has been \doxysectlink{intro_guide_intro_init}{initialized}{1}.

@wayland The Wayland protocol provides no way to check whether a window is iconfied, so \doxylink{group__window_ga39d44b7c056e55e581355a92d240b58a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+ICONIFIED} always returns {\ttfamily GLFW\+\_\+\+FALSE}.
\end{DoxyRemark}
@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
\doxysectlink{window_guide_window_attribs}{Window attributes}{2}

\Hypertarget{group__window_ga72718c983a9fffaa27f786bfe7d1c9ee}\index{Window reference@{Window reference}!glfwGetWindowContentScale@{glfwGetWindowContentScale}}
\index{glfwGetWindowContentScale@{glfwGetWindowContentScale}!Window reference@{Window reference}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwGetWindowContentScale()}{glfwGetWindowContentScale()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_ga72718c983a9fffaa27f786bfe7d1c9ee} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}} glfw\+Get\+Window\+Content\+Scale (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{window}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_a0d954e435550ebcb2035013bfea2db85}{float}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{xscale}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_a0d954e435550ebcb2035013bfea2db85}{float}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{yscale}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Retrieves the content scale for the specified window. 

This function retrieves the content scale for the specified window. The content scale is the ratio between the current DPI and the platform\textquotesingle{}s default DPI. This is especially important for text and any UI elements. If the pixel dimensions of your UI scaled by this look appropriate on your machine then it should appear at a reasonable size on other machines regardless of their DPI and scaling settings. This relies on the system DPI and scaling settings being somewhat correct.

On platforms where each monitors can have its own content scale, the window content scale will depend on which monitor the system considers the window to be on.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em window} & The window to query. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em xscale} & Where to store the x-\/axis content scale, or {\ttfamily NULL}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em yscale} & Where to store the y-\/axis content scale, or {\ttfamily NULL}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
@errors Possible errors include \doxylink{group__errors_ga2374ee02c177f12e1fa76ff3ed15e14a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED} and \doxylink{group__errors_gad44162d78100ea5e87cdd38426b8c7a1}{GLFW\+\_\+\+PLATFORM\+\_\+\+ERROR}.

@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
\doxysectlink{window_guide_window_scale}{Window content scale}{2}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\Hypertarget{group__window_gaad46cdaae2eb732f68d3a1499a7c5409}\index{Window reference@{Window reference}!glfwGetWindowFrameSize@{glfwGetWindowFrameSize}}
\index{glfwGetWindowFrameSize@{glfwGetWindowFrameSize}!Window reference@{Window reference}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwGetWindowFrameSize()}{glfwGetWindowFrameSize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_gaad46cdaae2eb732f68d3a1499a7c5409} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}} glfw\+Get\+Window\+Frame\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{window}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{left}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{top}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{right}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{bottom}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Retrieves the size of the frame of the window. 

This function retrieves the size, in screen coordinates, of each edge of the frame of the specified window. This size includes the title bar, if the window has one. The size of the frame may vary depending on the \doxysectlink{window_guide_window_hints_wnd}{window-\/related hints}{3} used to create it.

Because this function retrieves the size of each window frame edge and not the offset along a particular coordinate axis, the retrieved values will always be zero or positive.

Any or all of the size arguments may be {\ttfamily NULL}. If an error occurs, all non-\/{\ttfamily NULL} size arguments will be set to zero.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em window} & The window whose frame size to query. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em left} & Where to store the size, in screen coordinates, of the left edge of the window frame, or {\ttfamily NULL}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em top} & Where to store the size, in screen coordinates, of the top edge of the window frame, or {\ttfamily NULL}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em right} & Where to store the size, in screen coordinates, of the right edge of the window frame, or {\ttfamily NULL}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em bottom} & Where to store the size, in screen coordinates, of the bottom edge of the window frame, or {\ttfamily NULL}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
@errors Possible errors include \doxylink{group__errors_ga2374ee02c177f12e1fa76ff3ed15e14a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED} and \doxylink{group__errors_gad44162d78100ea5e87cdd38426b8c7a1}{GLFW\+\_\+\+PLATFORM\+\_\+\+ERROR}.

@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
\doxysectlink{window_guide_window_size}{Window size}{2}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxySince}{自从}
Added in version 3.\+1. 
\end{DoxySince}
\Hypertarget{group__window_gad441645a53bc9274a0ee163d40f0c637}\index{Window reference@{Window reference}!glfwGetWindowMonitor@{glfwGetWindowMonitor}}
\index{glfwGetWindowMonitor@{glfwGetWindowMonitor}!Window reference@{Window reference}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwGetWindowMonitor()}{glfwGetWindowMonitor()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_gad441645a53bc9274a0ee163d40f0c637} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group__monitor_ga8d9efd1cde9426692c73fe40437d0ae3}{GLFWmonitor}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} glfw\+Get\+Window\+Monitor (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{window}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns the monitor that the window uses for full screen mode. 

This function returns the handle of the monitor that the specified window is in full screen on.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em window} & The window to query. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
The monitor, or {\ttfamily NULL} if the window is in windowed mode or an \doxysectlink{intro_guide_error_handling}{error}{1} occurred.
\end{DoxyReturn}
@errors Possible errors include \doxylink{group__errors_ga2374ee02c177f12e1fa76ff3ed15e14a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}.

@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}

\Hypertarget{group__window_gad124d57a1c1c519f60c9765cd0c2a89c}\index{Window reference@{Window reference}!glfwGetWindowOpacity@{glfwGetWindowOpacity}}
\index{glfwGetWindowOpacity@{glfwGetWindowOpacity}!Window reference@{Window reference}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwGetWindowOpacity()}{glfwGetWindowOpacity()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_gad124d57a1c1c519f60c9765cd0c2a89c} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_a0d954e435550ebcb2035013bfea2db85}{float}} glfw\+Get\+Window\+Opacity (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{window}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns the opacity of the whole window. 

This function returns the opacity of the window, including any decorations.

The opacity (or alpha) value is a positive finite number between zero and one, where zero is fully transparent and one is fully opaque. If the system does not support whole window transparency, this function always returns one.

The initial opacity value for newly created windows is one.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em window} & The window to query. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
The opacity value of the specified window.
\end{DoxyReturn}
@errors Possible errors include \doxylink{group__errors_ga2374ee02c177f12e1fa76ff3ed15e14a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED} and \doxylink{group__errors_gad44162d78100ea5e87cdd38426b8c7a1}{GLFW\+\_\+\+PLATFORM\+\_\+\+ERROR}.

@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}

\Hypertarget{group__window_ga0076a8591ef7494d359730cf2250b45b}\index{Window reference@{Window reference}!glfwGetWindowPos@{glfwGetWindowPos}}
\index{glfwGetWindowPos@{glfwGetWindowPos}!Window reference@{Window reference}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwGetWindowPos()}{glfwGetWindowPos()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_ga0076a8591ef7494d359730cf2250b45b} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}} glfw\+Get\+Window\+Pos (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{window}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{xpos}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ypos}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Retrieves the position of the content area of the specified window. 

Retrieves the position of the client area of the specified window.

This function retrieves the position, in screen coordinates, of the upper-\/left corner of the content area of the specified window.

Any or all of the position arguments may be {\ttfamily NULL}. If an error occurs, all non-\/{\ttfamily NULL} position arguments will be set to zero.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em window} & The window to query. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em xpos} & Where to store the x-\/coordinate of the upper-\/left corner of the content area, or {\ttfamily NULL}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em ypos} & Where to store the y-\/coordinate of the upper-\/left corner of the content area, or {\ttfamily NULL}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
@errors Possible errors include \doxylink{group__errors_ga2374ee02c177f12e1fa76ff3ed15e14a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group__errors_gad44162d78100ea5e87cdd38426b8c7a1}{GLFW\+\_\+\+PLATFORM\+\_\+\+ERROR} and \doxylink{group__errors_ga526fba20a01504a8086c763b6ca53ce5}{GLFW\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+UNAVAILABLE} (see remarks).

\begin{DoxyRemark}{备注}
@wayland There is no way for an application to retrieve the global position of its windows. This function will emit \doxylink{group__errors_ga526fba20a01504a8086c763b6ca53ce5}{GLFW\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+UNAVAILABLE}.
\end{DoxyRemark}
@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwGetWindowSize()}{glfwGetWindowSize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_ga7feb769ebb3f3d21579b5a3fb07be76e} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}} glfw\+Get\+Window\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{window}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{width}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{height}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Retrieves the size of the content area of the specified window. 

Retrieves the size of the client area of the specified window.

This function retrieves the size, in screen coordinates, of the content area of the specified window. If you wish to retrieve the size of the framebuffer of the window in pixels, see \doxylink{group__window_gaf7d17f3534b4b6dc9a6f905e3a240b7e}{glfw\+Get\+Framebuffer\+Size}.

Any or all of the size arguments may be {\ttfamily NULL}. If an error occurs, all non-\/{\ttfamily NULL} size arguments will be set to zero.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em window} & The window whose size to retrieve. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em width} & Where to store the width, in screen coordinates, of the content area, or {\ttfamily NULL}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em height} & Where to store the height, in screen coordinates, of the content area, or {\ttfamily NULL}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
@errors Possible errors include \doxylink{group__errors_ga2374ee02c177f12e1fa76ff3ed15e14a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED} and \doxylink{group__errors_gad44162d78100ea5e87cdd38426b8c7a1}{GLFW\+\_\+\+PLATFORM\+\_\+\+ERROR}.

@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

\Hypertarget{group__window_ga950a05eb8b012928ffaecdd1d41a62b4}\index{Window reference@{Window reference}!glfwGetWindowTitle@{glfwGetWindowTitle}}
\index{glfwGetWindowTitle@{glfwGetWindowTitle}!Window reference@{Window reference}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwGetWindowTitle()}{glfwGetWindowTitle()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_ga950a05eb8b012928ffaecdd1d41a62b4} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} glfw\+Get\+Window\+Title (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{window}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns the title of the specified window. 

This function returns the window title, encoded as UTF-\/8, of the specified window. This is the title set previously by \doxylink{group__window_gaaccd00fafe81e2db94e8cdf55721e055}{glfw\+Create\+Window} or \doxylink{group__window_ga861ed3414ab8120e2f74151a666ed1dc}{glfw\+Set\+Window\+Title}.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em window} & The window to query. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
The UTF-\/8 encoded window title, or {\ttfamily NULL} if an \doxysectlink{intro_guide_error_handling}{error}{1} occurred.
\end{DoxyReturn}
@errors Possible errors include \doxylink{group__errors_ga2374ee02c177f12e1fa76ff3ed15e14a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{备注}
The returned title is currently a copy of the title last set by \doxylink{group__window_gaaccd00fafe81e2db94e8cdf55721e055}{glfw\+Create\+Window} or \doxylink{group__window_ga861ed3414ab8120e2f74151a666ed1dc}{glfw\+Set\+Window\+Title}. It does not include any additional text which may be appended by the platform or another program.
\end{DoxyRemark}
@pointer\+\_\+lifetime The returned string is allocated and freed by GLFW. You should not free it yourself. It is valid until the next call to \doxylink{group__window_ga950a05eb8b012928ffaecdd1d41a62b4}{glfw\+Get\+Window\+Title} or \doxylink{group__window_ga861ed3414ab8120e2f74151a666ed1dc}{glfw\+Set\+Window\+Title}, or until the library is terminated.

@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
\doxysectlink{window_guide_window_title}{Window title}{2} 

\doxylink{group__window_ga861ed3414ab8120e2f74151a666ed1dc}{glfw\+Set\+Window\+Title}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxySince}{自从}
Added in version 3.\+4. 
\end{DoxySince}

\Hypertarget{group__window_ga24274e3c6ecd44e11fec5e6b66e4d7f3}\index{Window reference@{Window reference}!glfwIconifyWindow@{glfwIconifyWindow}}
\index{glfwIconifyWindow@{glfwIconifyWindow}!Window reference@{Window reference}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwIconifyWindow()}{glfwIconifyWindow()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_ga24274e3c6ecd44e11fec5e6b66e4d7f3} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}} glfw\+Iconify\+Window (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{window}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Iconifies the specified window. 

This function iconifies (minimizes) the specified window if it was previously restored. If the window is already iconified, this function does nothing.

If the specified window is a full screen window, GLFW restores the original video mode of the monitor. The window\textquotesingle{}s desired video mode is set again when the window is restored.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em window} & The window to iconify.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
@errors Possible errors include \doxylink{group__errors_ga2374ee02c177f12e1fa76ff3ed15e14a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED} and \doxylink{group__errors_gad44162d78100ea5e87cdd38426b8c7a1}{GLFW\+\_\+\+PLATFORM\+\_\+\+ERROR}.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{备注}
@wayland Once a window is iconified, \doxylink{group__window_ga1e29caf0b819f578b04db52fff17256c}{glfw\+Restore\+Window} won’t be able to restore it. This is a design decision of the xdg-\/shell protocol.
\end{DoxyRemark}
@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
\doxysectlink{window_guide_window_iconify}{Window iconification}{2} 

\doxylink{group__window_ga1e29caf0b819f578b04db52fff17256c}{glfw\+Restore\+Window} 

\doxylink{group__window_ga4f825a55367d3fabde3d06e7f30128e8}{glfw\+Maximize\+Window}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxySince}{自从}
Added in version 2.\+1. @glfw3 Added window handle parameter.
\end{DoxySince}
This function iconifies (minimizes) the specified window if it was previously restored. If the window is already iconified, this function does nothing.

If the specified window is a full screen window, the original monitor resolution is restored until the window is restored.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em window} & The window to iconify.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
@errors Possible errors include \doxylink{group__errors_ga2374ee02c177f12e1fa76ff3ed15e14a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED} and \doxylink{group__errors_gad44162d78100ea5e87cdd38426b8c7a1}{GLFW\+\_\+\+PLATFORM\+\_\+\+ERROR}.

@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

\Hypertarget{group__window_ga872d16e4c77f58c0436f356255920cfc}\index{Window reference@{Window reference}!glfwPollEvents@{glfwPollEvents}}
\index{glfwPollEvents@{glfwPollEvents}!Window reference@{Window reference}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwPollEvents()}{glfwPollEvents()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_ga872d16e4c77f58c0436f356255920cfc} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}} glfw\+Poll\+Events (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}}}]{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Processes all pending events. 

This function processes only those events that are already in the event queue and then returns immediately. Processing events will cause the window and input callbacks associated with those events to be called.

On some platforms, a window move, resize or menu operation will cause event processing to block. This is due to how event processing is designed on those platforms. You can use the \doxysectlink{window_guide_window_refresh}{window refresh callback}{2} to redraw the contents of your window when necessary during such operations.

Do not assume that callbacks you set will {\itshape only} be called in response to event processing functions like this one. While it is necessary to poll for events, window systems that require GLFW to register callbacks of its own can pass events to GLFW in response to many window system function calls. GLFW will pass those events on to the application callbacks before returning.

Event processing is not required for joystick input to work.

@errors Possible errors include \doxylink{group__errors_ga2374ee02c177f12e1fa76ff3ed15e14a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED} and \doxylink{group__errors_gad44162d78100ea5e87cdd38426b8c7a1}{GLFW\+\_\+\+PLATFORM\+\_\+\+ERROR}.

@reentrancy This function must not be called from a callback.

@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
\doxysectlink{input_guide_events}{Event processing}{1} 

\doxylink{group__window_ga6e042d05823c11e11c7339b81a237738}{glfw\+Wait\+Events} 

\doxylink{group__window_ga05223a0a4c5e50f10f289e60398153aa}{glfw\+Wait\+Events\+Timeout}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxySince}{自从}
Added in version 1.\+0.
\end{DoxySince}
This function processes only those events that are already in the event queue and then returns immediately. Processing events will cause the window and input callbacks associated with those events to be called.

On some platforms, a window move, resize or menu operation will cause event processing to block. This is due to how event processing is designed on those platforms. You can use the \doxysectlink{window_guide_window_refresh}{window refresh callback}{2} to redraw the contents of your window when necessary during such operations.

On some platforms, certain events are sent directly to the application without going through the event queue, causing callbacks to be called outside of a call to one of the event processing functions.

Event processing is not required for joystick input to work.

@errors Possible errors include \doxylink{group__errors_ga2374ee02c177f12e1fa76ff3ed15e14a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED} and \doxylink{group__errors_gad44162d78100ea5e87cdd38426b8c7a1}{GLFW\+\_\+\+PLATFORM\+\_\+\+ERROR}.

@reentrancy This function must not be called from a callback.

@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}

Posts an empty event to the event queue. 

This function posts an empty event from the current thread to the event queue, causing \doxylink{group__window_ga6e042d05823c11e11c7339b81a237738}{glfw\+Wait\+Events} or \doxylink{group__window_ga05223a0a4c5e50f10f289e60398153aa}{glfw\+Wait\+Events\+Timeout} to return.

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

This function posts an empty event from the current thread to the event queue, causing \doxylink{group__window_ga6e042d05823c11e11c7339b81a237738}{glfw\+Wait\+Events} to return.

If no windows exist, this function returns immediately. For synchronization of threads in applications that do not create windows, use your threading library of choice.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwRequestWindowAttention()}{glfwRequestWindowAttention()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_gad0c9629abb49447bedd28080642b8538} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}} glfw\+Request\+Window\+Attention (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{window}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Requests user attention to the specified window. 

This function requests user attention to the specified window. On platforms where this is not supported, attention is requested to the application as a whole.

Once the user has given attention, usually by focusing the window or application, the system will end the request automatically.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em window} & The window to request attention to.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRemark}{备注}
@macos Attention is requested to the application as a whole, not the specific window.
\end{DoxyRemark}
@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

Restores the specified window. 

This function restores the specified window if it was previously iconified (minimized) or maximized. If the window is already restored, this function does nothing.

If the specified window is an iconified full screen window, its desired video mode is set again for its monitor when the window is restored.

\Hypertarget{group__window_gad2ae94a2c5ee1c46a36e13a8f4ac68ac}\index{Window reference@{Window reference}!glfwSetWindowAspectRatio@{glfwSetWindowAspectRatio}}
\index{glfwSetWindowAspectRatio@{glfwSetWindowAspectRatio}!Window reference@{Window reference}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwSetWindowAspectRatio()}{glfwSetWindowAspectRatio()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_gad2ae94a2c5ee1c46a36e13a8f4ac68ac} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}} glfw\+Set\+Window\+Aspect\+Ratio (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{window}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}}}]{numer}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}}}]{denom}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the aspect ratio of the specified window. 

This function sets the required aspect ratio of the content area of the specified window. If the window is full screen, the aspect ratio only takes effect once it is made windowed. If the window is not resizable, this function does nothing.

The aspect ratio is specified as a numerator and a denominator and both values must be greater than zero. For example, the common 16\+:9 aspect ratio is specified as 16 and 9, respectively.

If the numerator and denominator is set to {\ttfamily GLFW\+\_\+\+DONT\+\_\+\+CARE} then the aspect ratio limit is disabled.

The aspect ratio is applied immediately to a windowed mode window and may cause it to be resized.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em window} & The window to set limits for. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em numer} & The numerator of the desired aspect ratio, or {\ttfamily GLFW\+\_\+\+DONT\+\_\+\+CARE}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em denom} & The denominator of the desired aspect ratio, or {\ttfamily GLFW\+\_\+\+DONT\+\_\+\+CARE}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
@errors Possible errors include \doxylink{group__errors_ga2374ee02c177f12e1fa76ff3ed15e14a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group__errors_gaaf2ef9aa8202c2b82ac2d921e554c687}{GLFW\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} and \doxylink{group__errors_gad44162d78100ea5e87cdd38426b8c7a1}{GLFW\+\_\+\+PLATFORM\+\_\+\+ERROR}.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{备注}
If you set size limits and an aspect ratio that conflict, the results are undefined.

@wayland The aspect ratio will not be applied until the window is actually resized, either by the user or by the compositor.
\end{DoxyRemark}
@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
\doxysectlink{window_guide_window_sizelimits}{Window size limits}{2} 

\doxylink{group__window_ga8af814fc98d786d1de2505b40b707de8}{glfw\+Set\+Window\+Size\+Limits}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxySince}{自从}
Added in version 3.\+2.
\end{DoxySince}
This function sets the required aspect ratio of the client area of the specified window. If the window is full screen, the aspect ratio only takes effect once it is made windowed. If the window is not resizable, this function does nothing.

The aspect ratio is specified as a numerator and a denominator and both values must be greater than zero. For example, the common 16\+:9 aspect ratio is specified as 16 and 9, respectively.

If the numerator and denominator is set to {\ttfamily GLFW\+\_\+\+DONT\+\_\+\+CARE} then the aspect ratio limit is disabled.

The aspect ratio is applied immediately to a windowed mode window and may cause it to be resized.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em window} & The window to set limits for. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em numer} & The numerator of the desired aspect ratio, or {\ttfamily GLFW\+\_\+\+DONT\+\_\+\+CARE}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em denom} & The denominator of the desired aspect ratio, or {\ttfamily GLFW\+\_\+\+DONT\+\_\+\+CARE}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
@errors Possible errors include \doxylink{group__errors_ga2374ee02c177f12e1fa76ff3ed15e14a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group__errors_gaaf2ef9aa8202c2b82ac2d921e554c687}{GLFW\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE} and \doxylink{group__errors_gad44162d78100ea5e87cdd38426b8c7a1}{GLFW\+\_\+\+PLATFORM\+\_\+\+ERROR}.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{备注}
If you set size limits and an aspect ratio that conflict, the results are undefined.
\end{DoxyRemark}
@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

\Hypertarget{group__window_gad39f43f07856efcf3d656426a9284c75}\index{Window reference@{Window reference}!glfwSetWindowAttrib@{glfwSetWindowAttrib}}
\index{glfwSetWindowAttrib@{glfwSetWindowAttrib}!Window reference@{Window reference}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwSetWindowAttrib()}{glfwSetWindowAttrib()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_gad39f43f07856efcf3d656426a9284c75} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}} glfw\+Set\+Window\+Attrib (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{window}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}}}]{attrib}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}}}]{value}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets an attribute of the specified window. 

This function sets the value of an attribute of the specified window.

The supported attributes are \doxylink{window_guide_GLFW_DECORATED_attrib}{GLFW\+\_\+\+DECORATED}, \doxylink{window_guide_GLFW_RESIZABLE_attrib}{GLFW\+\_\+\+RESIZABLE}, \doxylink{window_guide_GLFW_FLOATING_attrib}{GLFW\+\_\+\+FLOATING}, \doxylink{window_guide_GLFW_AUTO_ICONIFY_attrib}{GLFW\+\_\+\+AUTO\+\_\+\+ICONIFY} and \doxylink{window_guide_GLFW_FOCUS_ON_SHOW_attrib}{GLFW\+\_\+\+FOCUS\+\_\+\+ON\+\_\+\+SHOW}. \doxylink{window_guide_GLFW_MOUSE_PASSTHROUGH_attrib}{GLFW\+\_\+\+MOUSE\+\_\+\+PASSTHROUGH}

Some of these attributes are ignored for full screen windows. The new value will take effect if the window is later made windowed.

Some of these attributes are ignored for windowed mode windows. The new value will take effect if the window is later made full screen.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em window} & The window to set the attribute for. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em attrib} & A supported window attribute. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em value} & {\ttfamily GLFW\+\_\+\+TRUE} or {\ttfamily GLFW\+\_\+\+FALSE}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
@errors Possible errors include \doxylink{group__errors_ga2374ee02c177f12e1fa76ff3ed15e14a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group__errors_ga76f6bb9c4eea73db675f096b404593ce}{GLFW\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+ENUM}, \doxylink{group__errors_gaaf2ef9aa8202c2b82ac2d921e554c687}{GLFW\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}, \doxylink{group__errors_gad44162d78100ea5e87cdd38426b8c7a1}{GLFW\+\_\+\+PLATFORM\+\_\+\+ERROR} and \doxylink{group__errors_ga526fba20a01504a8086c763b6ca53ce5}{GLFW\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+UNAVAILABLE} (see remarks).

\begin{DoxyRemark}{备注}
Calling \doxylink{group__window_ga1bb0c7e100418e284dbb800789c63d40}{glfw\+Get\+Window\+Attrib} will always return the latest value, even if that value is ignored by the current mode of the window.

@wayland The \doxylink{window_guide_GLFW_FLOATING_attrib}{GLFW\+\_\+\+FLOATING} window attribute is not supported. Setting this will emit \doxylink{group__errors_ga526fba20a01504a8086c763b6ca53ce5}{GLFW\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+UNAVAILABLE}.
\end{DoxyRemark}
@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwSetWindowCloseCallback()}{glfwSetWindowCloseCallback()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_ga693d778815971a06e1a5a7bcdeff3d36} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_gabf859b936d80961b7d39013a9694cc3e}{GLFWwindowclosefun}} glfw\+Set\+Window\+Close\+Callback (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{window}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_gabf859b936d80961b7d39013a9694cc3e}{GLFWwindowclosefun}}}]{callback}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the close callback for the specified window. 

This function sets the close callback of the specified window, which is called when the user attempts to close the window, for example by clicking the close widget in the title bar.

The close flag is set before this callback is called, but you can modify it at any time with \doxylink{group__window_ga1cadeda7a1e2f224e06a8415d30741aa}{glfw\+Set\+Window\+Should\+Close}.

The close callback is not triggered by \doxylink{group__window_ga806747476b7247d292be3711c323ea10}{glfw\+Destroy\+Window}.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em window} & The window whose callback to set. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em callback} & The new callback, or {\ttfamily NULL} to remove the currently set callback. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
The previously set callback, or {\ttfamily NULL} if no callback was set or the library had not been \doxysectlink{intro_guide_intro_init}{initialized}{1}.
\end{DoxyReturn}
@callback\+\_\+signature

\end{DoxyCode}
 For more information about the callback parameters, see the \doxylink{group__window_gabf859b936d80961b7d39013a9694cc3e}{function pointer type}.

\end{DoxyRemark}

\Hypertarget{group__window_gacce1c4dd273b5c4c60b05599f8725b4e}\index{Window reference@{Window reference}!glfwSetWindowFocusCallback@{glfwSetWindowFocusCallback}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwSetWindowFocusCallback()}{glfwSetWindowFocusCallback()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_gacce1c4dd273b5c4c60b05599f8725b4e} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_gabc58c47e9d93f6eb1862d615c3680f46}{GLFWwindowfocusfun}} glfw\+Set\+Window\+Focus\+Callback (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{window}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_gabc58c47e9d93f6eb1862d615c3680f46}{GLFWwindowfocusfun}}}]{callback}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the focus callback for the specified window. 

This function sets the focus callback of the specified window, which is called when the window gains or loses input focus.

After the focus callback is called for a window that lost input focus, synthetic key and mouse button release events will be generated for all such that had been pressed. For more information, see \doxylink{group__input_gaa4cbcb81b939b8800e44cea971ddae47}{glfw\+Set\+Key\+Callback} and \doxylink{group__input_gab8f17646f43cdca14e5095512618fdf6}{glfw\+Set\+Mouse\+Button\+Callback}.

\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{group__window_ga182987a1a62a41a924842b9473d560df}\index{Window reference@{Window reference}!glfwSetWindowIcon@{glfwSetWindowIcon}}
\index{glfwSetWindowIcon@{glfwSetWindowIcon}!Window reference@{Window reference}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwSetWindowIcon()}{glfwSetWindowIcon()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_ga182987a1a62a41a924842b9473d560df} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}} glfw\+Set\+Window\+Icon (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{window}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}}}]{count}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_g_l_f_wimage}{GLFWimage}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{images}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the icon for the specified window. 

This function sets the icon of the specified window. If passed an array of candidate images, those of or closest to the sizes desired by the system are selected. If no images are specified, the window reverts to its default icon.

The pixels are 32-\/bit, little-\/endian, non-\/premultiplied RGBA, i.\+e. eight bits per channel with the red channel first. They are arranged canonically as packed sequential rows, starting from the top-\/left corner.

The desired image sizes varies depending on platform and system settings. The selected images will be rescaled as needed. Good sizes include 16x16, 32x32 and 48x48.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em window} & The window whose icon to set. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em count} & The number of images in the specified array, or zero to revert to the default window icon. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em images} & The images to create the icon from. This is ignored if count is zero.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
@errors Possible errors include \doxylink{group__errors_ga2374ee02c177f12e1fa76ff3ed15e14a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group__errors_gaaf2ef9aa8202c2b82ac2d921e554c687}{GLFW\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+VALUE}, \doxylink{group__errors_gad44162d78100ea5e87cdd38426b8c7a1}{GLFW\+\_\+\+PLATFORM\+\_\+\+ERROR} and \doxylink{group__errors_ga526fba20a01504a8086c763b6ca53ce5}{GLFW\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+UNAVAILABLE} (see remarks).

@pointer\+\_\+lifetime The specified image data is copied before this function returns.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{备注}
@macos Regular windows do not have icons on mac\+OS. This function will emit \doxylink{group__errors_ga526fba20a01504a8086c763b6ca53ce5}{GLFW\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+UNAVAILABLE}. The dock icon will be the same as the application bundle\textquotesingle{}s icon. For more information on bundles, see the \href{https://developer.apple.com/library/mac/documentation/CoreFoundation/Conceptual/CFBundles/}{\texttt{ Bundle Programming Guide}} in the Mac Developer Library.

@wayland There is no existing protocol to change an icon, the window will thus inherit the one defined in the application\textquotesingle{}s desktop file. This function will emit \doxylink{group__errors_ga526fba20a01504a8086c763b6ca53ce5}{GLFW\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+UNAVAILABLE}.
\end{DoxyRemark}
@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
\doxysectlink{window_guide_window_icon}{Window icon}{2}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxySince}{自从}
Added in version 3.\+2.
\end{DoxySince}
This function sets the icon of the specified window. If passed an array of candidate images, those of or closest to the sizes desired by the system are selected. If no images are specified, the window reverts to its default icon.

The desired image sizes varies depending on platform and system settings. The selected images will be rescaled as needed. Good sizes include 16x16, 32x32 and 48x48.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em window} & The window whose icon to set. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em count} & The number of images in the specified array, or zero to revert to the default window icon. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em images} & The images to create the icon from. This is ignored if count is zero.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
@errors Possible errors include \doxylink{group__errors_ga2374ee02c177f12e1fa76ff3ed15e14a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED} and \doxylink{group__errors_gad44162d78100ea5e87cdd38426b8c7a1}{GLFW\+\_\+\+PLATFORM\+\_\+\+ERROR}.

@pointer\+\_\+lifetime The specified image data is copied before this function returns.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{备注}
@osx The GLFW window has no icon, as it is not a document window, but the dock icon will be the same as the application bundle\textquotesingle{}s icon. For more information on bundles, see the \href{https://developer.apple.com/library/mac/documentation/CoreFoundation/Conceptual/CFBundles/}{\texttt{ Bundle Programming Guide}} in the Mac Developer Library.
\end{DoxyRemark}
@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\end{DoxySince}

\Hypertarget{group__window_ga3e9f355edb6b9247149ddea2335eda69}\index{Window reference@{Window reference}!glfwSetWindowIconifyCallback@{glfwSetWindowIconifyCallback}}
\index{glfwSetWindowIconifyCallback@{glfwSetWindowIconifyCallback}!Window reference@{Window reference}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwSetWindowIconifyCallback()}{glfwSetWindowIconifyCallback()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_ga3e9f355edb6b9247149ddea2335eda69}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}

\Hypertarget{group__window_ga12fabf78575e59c00f822f323ae0b6ae}\index{Window reference@{Window reference}!glfwSetWindowMonitor@{glfwSetWindowMonitor}}
\index{glfwSetWindowMonitor@{glfwSetWindowMonitor}!Window reference@{Window reference}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwSetWindowMonitor()}{glfwSetWindowMonitor()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_ga12fabf78575e59c00f822f323ae0b6ae} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}} glfw\+Set\+Window\+Monitor (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{window}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__monitor_ga8d9efd1cde9426692c73fe40437d0ae3}{GLFWmonitor}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{monitor}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}}}]{xpos}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}}}]{ypos}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}}}]{width}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}}}]{height}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}}}]{refresh\+Rate}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the mode, monitor, video mode and placement of a window. 

This function sets the monitor that the window uses for full screen mode or, if the monitor is {\ttfamily NULL}, makes it windowed mode.

When setting a monitor, this function updates the width, height and refresh rate of the desired video mode and switches to the video mode closest to it. The window position is ignored when setting a monitor.

When the monitor is {\ttfamily NULL}, the position, width and height are used to place the window content area. The refresh rate is ignored when no monitor is specified.

If you only wish to update the resolution of a full screen window or the size of a windowed mode window, see \doxylink{group__window_gae54d1f4915ded15e267ddd3f41496cd2}{glfw\+Set\+Window\+Size}.

When a window transitions from full screen to windowed mode, this function restores any previous window settings such as whether it is decorated, floating, resizable, has size or aspect ratio limits, etc.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em window} & The window whose monitor, size or video mode to set. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em monitor} & The desired monitor, or {\ttfamily NULL} to set windowed mode. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em xpos} & The desired x-\/coordinate of the upper-\/left corner of the content area. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em ypos} & The desired y-\/coordinate of the upper-\/left corner of the content area. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em width} & The desired with, in screen coordinates, of the content area or video mode. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em height} & The desired height, in screen coordinates, of the content area or video mode. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em refresh\+Rate} & The desired refresh rate, in Hz, of the video mode, or {\ttfamily GLFW\+\_\+\+DONT\+\_\+\+CARE}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
@errors Possible errors include \doxylink{group__errors_ga2374ee02c177f12e1fa76ff3ed15e14a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED} and \doxylink{group__errors_gad44162d78100ea5e87cdd38426b8c7a1}{GLFW\+\_\+\+PLATFORM\+\_\+\+ERROR}.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{备注}
The Open\+GL or Open\+GL ES context will not be destroyed or otherwise affected by any resizing or mode switching, although you may need to update your viewport if the framebuffer size has changed.

@wayland The desired window position is ignored, as there is no way for an application to set this property.
\end{DoxyRemark}
@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}

\Hypertarget{group__window_ga62a784fe328f227727cbcd0d07480ff3}\index{Window reference@{Window reference}!glfwSetWindowOpacity@{glfwSetWindowOpacity}}
\index{glfwSetWindowOpacity@{glfwSetWindowOpacity}!Window reference@{Window reference}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwSetWindowOpacity()}{glfwSetWindowOpacity()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_ga62a784fe328f227727cbcd0d07480ff3} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}} glfw\+Set\+Window\+Opacity (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{window}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_a0d954e435550ebcb2035013bfea2db85}{float}}}]{opacity}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the opacity of the whole window. 

This function sets the opacity of the window, including any decorations.

The opacity (or alpha) value is a positive finite number between zero and one, where zero is fully transparent and one is fully opaque.

The initial opacity value for newly created windows is one.

A window created with framebuffer transparency may not use whole window transparency. The results of doing this are undefined.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em window} & The window to set the opacity for. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em opacity} & The desired opacity of the specified window.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
@errors Possible errors include \doxylink{group__errors_ga2374ee02c177f12e1fa76ff3ed15e14a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group__errors_gad44162d78100ea5e87cdd38426b8c7a1}{GLFW\+\_\+\+PLATFORM\+\_\+\+ERROR} and \doxylink{group__errors_ga526fba20a01504a8086c763b6ca53ce5}{GLFW\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+UNAVAILABLE} (see remarks).

\begin{DoxyRemark}{备注}
@wayland There is no way to set an opacity factor for a window. This function will emit \doxylink{group__errors_ga526fba20a01504a8086c763b6ca53ce5}{GLFW\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+UNAVAILABLE}.
\end{DoxyRemark}
@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

\Hypertarget{group__window_ga0dc8d880a0d87be16d3ea8114561f6f0}\index{Window reference@{Window reference}!glfwSetWindowPos@{glfwSetWindowPos}}
\index{glfwSetWindowPos@{glfwSetWindowPos}!Window reference@{Window reference}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwSetWindowPos()}{glfwSetWindowPos()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_ga0dc8d880a0d87be16d3ea8114561f6f0} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc_8h_a9d6d8aef94ac19034a5f163606f84830}{void}} glfw\+Set\+Window\+Pos (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{window}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}}}]{xpos}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae88a82478e3818cade3f598c25437904}{int}}}]{ypos}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the position of the content area of the specified window. 

Sets the position of the client area of the specified window.

This function sets the position, in screen coordinates, of the upper-\/left corner of the content area of the specified windowed mode window. If the window is a full screen window, this function does nothing.

{\bfseries{Do not use this function}} to move an already visible window unless you have very good reasons for doing so, as it will confuse and annoy the user.

The window manager may put limits on what positions are allowed. GLFW cannot and should not override these limits.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em window} & The window to query. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em xpos} & The x-\/coordinate of the upper-\/left corner of the content area. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em ypos} & The y-\/coordinate of the upper-\/left corner of the content area.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
@errors Possible errors include \doxylink{group__errors_ga2374ee02c177f12e1fa76ff3ed15e14a}{GLFW\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+INITIALIZED}, \doxylink{group__errors_gad44162d78100ea5e87cdd38426b8c7a1}{GLFW\+\_\+\+PLATFORM\+\_\+\+ERROR} and \doxylink{group__errors_ga526fba20a01504a8086c763b6ca53ce5}{GLFW\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+UNAVAILABLE} (see remarks).

\begin{DoxyRemark}{备注}
@wayland There is no way for an application to set the global position of its windows. This function will emit \doxylink{group__errors_ga526fba20a01504a8086c763b6ca53ce5}{GLFW\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+UNAVAILABLE}.
\end{DoxyRemark}
@thread\+\_\+safety This function must only be called from the main thread.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{glfwSetWindowRefreshCallback()}{glfwSetWindowRefreshCallback()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__window_ga62bfa902c07a03b8ad9be37da31a4be7} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{glfw_2include_2_g_l_f_w_2glfw3_8h_a56da5036b2cc259351ae22fd6439bb47}{GLFWAPI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga431663a1427d2eb3a273bc398b6737b5}{GLFWwindowrefreshfun}} glfw\+Set\+Window\+Refresh\+Callback (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga3c96d80d363e67d13a41b5d1821f3242}{GLFWwindow}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{window}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__window_ga431663a1427d2eb3a273bc398b6737b5}{GLFWwindowrefreshfun}}}]{callback}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the refresh callback for the specified window. 

This function sets the refresh callback of the specified window, which is called when the content area of the window needs to be redrawn, for example if the window has been exposed after having been covered by another window.

On compositing window systems such as Aero, Compiz, Aqua or Wayland, where the window contents are saved off-\/screen, this callback may be called only very infrequently or never at all.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em window} & The window whose callback to set. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em callback} & The new callback, or {\ttfamily NULL} to remove the currently set callback. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
The previously set callback, or {\ttfamily NULL} if no callback was set or the library had not been \doxysectlink{intro_guide_intro_init}{initialized}{1}.
\end{DoxyReturn}
@callback\+\_\+signature

\end{DoxyCode}
 For more information about the callback parameters, see the \doxylink{group__window_ga431663a1427d2eb3a273bc398b6737b5}{function pointer type}.
